## 🔍 Cross-Page Patterns: Common HTML Issues

These HTML patterns cause the same accessibility errors across multiple pages. **Fix the pattern once in your codebase to fix it everywhere!**

### 🎯 Top Patterns to Fix (Highest Impact)

#### Pattern 1: Affects 54 page(s) - 54 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: ALFA
**Rule**: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)
**Issue**: Target has insufficient size

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<a href="https://de-de.facebook.com/bayern/" title="die Bayerische Staatskanzlei auf Facebook" target="_blank">...</a>
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
/a
```

**How to Replicate**:
1. Open any affected page in your browser
2. Press F12 to open DevTools
3. Go to Console tab
4. Run: `$x('/a')`
5. The element will be highlighted

**Affected Pages**:
- https://bayern.de/
- https://bayern.de/erklaerung-zur-barrierefreiheit/
- https://bayern.de/buergerservice/apps-messenger-rss/
- https://bayern.de/buergerservice/broschueren/
- https://bayern.de/buergerservice/buergerbeauftragter/
- *...and 49 more page(s)*

#### Pattern 11: Affects 54 page(s) - 54 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: ALFA
**Rule**: [SIA-R14: Images have an accessible name or are decorative](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r14)
**Issue**: The visible text content of the element is not included within its accessible name

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<a class="openNav" role="button" tabindex="0" aria-label="Menu aufklappen" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false">...</a>
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
/a[@class="openNav"]
```

**How to Replicate**:
1. Open any affected page in your browser
2. Press F12 to open DevTools
3. Go to Console tab
4. Run: `$x('/a[@class="openNav"]')`
5. The element will be highlighted

**Affected Pages**:

- https://bayern.de/buergerservice/broschueren/
- https://bayern.de/buergerservice/buergerbeauftragter/

## Detailed Failure Information (ALFA)

### https://bayern.de/

#### Rule: [SIA-R11: Button elements have an accessible name](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r11)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The link does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<a href="/eu-finanzen-power-regions-fordern-mehr-mitsprache-und-beteiligung-europaminister-beisswenger-auch-starke-standorte-unterliegen-transformationsprozessen/" target="_self">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="openNav" role="button" tabindex="0" aria-label="Menu aufklappen" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="openNav"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a tabindex="0" role="button" class="openSearch" aria-label="Suche starten" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="openSearch"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="/bericht-aus-der-kabinettssitzung-vom-10-maerz-2026/">Zum Bericht aus der Kabinettssitzung vom 10. März ...</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-prev disabled">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="owl-prev disabled"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-next">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="owl-next"]`

*... and 1 more failures for this rule*

#### Rule: [SIA-R14: Images have an accessible name or are decorative](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r14)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The visible text content of the element is not included within its accessible name
- HTML: `<a class="openNav" role="button" tabindex="0" aria-label="Menu aufklappen" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="openNav"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R18: ARIA states are consistent with element semantics](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r18)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The attribute is prohibited for the element on which it is specified

#### Rule: [SIA-R2: HTML elements have a valid lang attribute](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r2)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The image does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/uploads/2021/02/Facebook.png" class="sidebar-img" width="36" height="36" />`
- XPath: `/img[@class="sidebar-img"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The image does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/uploads/2021/09/Messenger_Icon_2X.png" class="notify-img " width="26" height="27" />`
- XPath: `/img[@class="notify-img "]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R3: lang attribute has a valid language code](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r3)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<li id="id-menu-level-2-child-7" class="nav-item level-2 has-child  " data-child="menu-level-2-child-7">...</li>`
- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-7"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<ul id="id-menu-level-2-child-7" aria-hidden="true" role="menu" class="navbar-nav flex-column menu-level menu-level-2 menu-level-2-child-7" data-level="2">...</ul>`
- XPath: `/ul[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-7"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<li id="id-menu-level-2-child-8" class="nav-item level-2 has-child  " data-child="menu-level-2-child-8">...</li>`
- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-8"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<ul id="id-menu-level-2-child-8" aria-hidden="true" role="menu" class="navbar-nav flex-column menu-level menu-level-2 menu-level-2-child-8" data-level="2">...</ul>`
- XPath: `/ul[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-8"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<li id="id-menu-level-2-child-10" class="nav-item level-2 has-child  " data-child="menu-level-2-child-10">...</li>`
- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-10"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R74](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r74)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="article-date">...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="article-date"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="count-subtitle">                                                Eu...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="count-subtitle"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="count-text">...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="count-text"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="media-date">10.03.2026</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="media-date"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R86: Page has a mechanism to bypass repeated blocks of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r86)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element is marked as decorative but is exposed
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-prev disabled">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="owl-prev disabled"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The element is marked as decorative but is exposed
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-next">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="owl-next"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The element is marked as decorative but is exposed
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-prev">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="owl-prev"]`

- HTML: `<a class="openNav" role="button" tabindex="0" aria-label="Menu aufklappen" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false">...</a>`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a tabindex="0" role="button" class="openSearch" aria-label="Suche starten" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="openSearch"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="#messenger">                                         Messenger...</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="#" class="close-mail">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="close-mail"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R14: Images have an accessible name or are decorative](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r14)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The visible text content of the element is not included within its accessible name
- HTML: `<a class="openNav" role="button" tabindex="0" aria-label="Menu aufklappen" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="openNav"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R18: ARIA states are consistent with element semantics](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r18)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The attribute is prohibited for the element on which it is specified

#### Rule: [SIA-R2: HTML elements have a valid lang attribute](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r2)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The image does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/uploads/2021/02/Facebook.png" class="sidebar-img" width="36" height="36" />`
- XPath: `/img[@class="sidebar-img"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The image does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/uploads/2021/09/Messenger_Icon_2X.png" class="notify-img " width="26" height="27" />`
- XPath: `/img[@class="notify-img "]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R3: lang attribute has a valid language code](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r3)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<li id="id-menu-level-2-child-7" class="nav-item level-2 has-child  " data-child="menu-level-2-child-7">...</li>`
- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-7"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<ul id="id-menu-level-2-child-7" aria-hidden="true" role="menu" class="navbar-nav flex-column menu-level menu-level-2 menu-level-2-child-7" data-level="2">...</ul>`
- XPath: `/ul[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-7"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<li id="id-menu-level-2-child-8" class="nav-item level-2 has-child  " data-child="menu-level-2-child-8">...</li>`
- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-8"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<ul id="id-menu-level-2-child-8" aria-hidden="true" role="menu" class="navbar-nav flex-column menu-level menu-level-2 menu-level-2-child-8" data-level="2">...</ul>`
- XPath: `/ul[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-8"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<li id="id-menu-level-2-child-10" class="nav-item level-2 has-child active current-ancestor" data-child="menu-level-2-child-10">...</li>`
- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-10"]`

- Message: The visible text content of the element is not included within its accessible name
- HTML: `<a class="openNav" role="button" tabindex="0" aria-label="Menu aufklappen" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="openNav"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R2: HTML elements have a valid lang attribute](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r2)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The image does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/uploads/2021/02/Facebook.png" class="sidebar-img" width="36" height="36" />`
- XPath: `/img[@class="sidebar-img"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The image does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/uploads/2021/09/Messenger_Icon_2X.png" class="notify-img " width="26" height="27" />`
- XPath: `/img[@class="notify-img "]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R3: lang attribute has a valid language code](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r3)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<li id="id-menu-level-2-child-7" class="nav-item level-2 has-child  " data-child="menu-level-2-child-7">...</li>`
- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-7"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<ul id="id-menu-level-2-child-7" aria-hidden="true" role="menu" class="navbar-nav flex-column menu-level menu-level-2 menu-level-2-child-7" data-level="2">...</ul>`
- XPath: `/ul[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-7"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<li id="id-menu-level-2-child-8" class="nav-item level-2 has-child  " data-child="menu-level-2-child-8">...</li>`
- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-8"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<ul id="id-menu-level-2-child-8" aria-hidden="true" role="menu" class="navbar-nav flex-column menu-level menu-level-2 menu-level-2-child-8" data-level="2">...</ul>`
- XPath: `/ul[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-8"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<li id="id-menu-level-2-child-10" class="nav-item level-2 has-child active current-ancestor" data-child="menu-level-2-child-10">...</li>`
- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-10"]`

- XPath: `/p[@class="contact-info-number"]`

- XPath: `/p[@class="contact-text"]`

- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="contact-celebrate-email" tabindex="0">...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="contact-celebrate-email"]`

- HTML: `<h2>Die Staatsministerien in den Sozialen Netzwerken</h2>`
- XPath: `/h2`

#### Rule: [SIA-R86: Page has a mechanism to bypass repeated blocks of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r86)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element is marked as decorative but is exposed
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-prev disabled">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="owl-prev disabled"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The element is marked as decorative but is exposed
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-next">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="owl-next"]`

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height of the paragraph is less than 1.5
- HTML: `<p>...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

#### Rule: [SIA-R74](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r74)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="sub-block-ribbon no-mar-bottom mar-top-18">Paul Kirchhof, ehemaliger Bundesverfassungsrichter</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="sub-block-ribbon no-mar-bottom mar-top-18"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="pdf-file">MP3, 2.02 MB</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="pdf-file"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R86: Page has a mechanism to bypass repeated blocks of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r86)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element is marked as decorative but is exposed
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-prev disabled">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="owl-prev disabled"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The element is marked as decorative but is exposed
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-next">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="owl-next"]`

- HTML: `<a class="openNav" role="button" tabindex="0" aria-label="Menu aufklappen" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="openNav"]`

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The attribute is prohibited for the element on which it is specified

#### Rule: [SIA-R74](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r74)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="sub-block-ribbon no-mar-bottom mar-top-18">Ministerpräsident Dr. Markus Söder (MdL)</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="sub-block-ribbon no-mar-bottom mar-top-18"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R86: Page has a mechanism to bypass repeated blocks of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r86)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element is marked as decorative but is exposed
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-prev disabled">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="owl-prev disabled"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The element is marked as decorative but is exposed
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-next">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="owl-next"]`

### https://bayern.de/presse/archiv-pressemitteilungen/

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="openNav" role="button" tabindex="0" aria-label="Menu aufklappen" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="openNav"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a tabindex="0" role="button" class="openSearch" aria-label="Suche starten" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="openSearch"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size

- XPath: `/a`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="#" class="close-mail">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="close-mail"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R12: Links have an accessible name](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r12)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The button does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<button class="btn btn-primary" type="submit" id="suchbutton">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@id="suchbutton"]`

- XPath: `/a[@class="openNav"]`

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The attribute is prohibited for the element on which it is specified

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The image does not have an accessible name

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The image does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/uploads/2021/09/Messenger_Icon_2X.png" class="notify-img " width="26" height="27" />`
- XPath: `/img[@class="notify-img "]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R3: lang attribute has a valid language code](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r3)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<li id="id-menu-level-2-child-7" class="nav-item level-2 has-child  " data-child="menu-level-2-child-7">...</li>`
- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-7"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<ul id="id-menu-level-2-child-7" aria-hidden="true" role="menu" class="navbar-nav flex-column menu-level menu-level-2 menu-level-2-child-7" data-level="2">...</ul>`
- XPath: `/ul[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-7"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<li id="id-menu-level-2-child-8" class="nav-item level-2 has-child  " data-child="menu-level-2-child-8">...</li>`
- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-8"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<ul id="id-menu-level-2-child-8" aria-hidden="true" role="menu" class="navbar-nav flex-column menu-level menu-level-2 menu-level-2-child-8" data-level="2">...</ul>`
- XPath: `/ul[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-8"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<li id="id-menu-level-2-child-10" class="nav-item level-2 has-child  " data-child="menu-level-2-child-10">...</li>`
- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-10"]`

- HTML: `<a href="/auftaktsitzung-des-neukonzipierten-bayerischen-ethikrates/">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="openNav" role="button" tabindex="0" aria-label="Menu aufklappen" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="openNav"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a tabindex="0" role="button" class="openSearch" aria-label="Suche starten" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="openSearch"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="#aufgaben">                                         Aufgaben ...</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="#" class="close-mail">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="close-mail"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R14: Images have an accessible name or are decorative](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r14)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The visible text content of the element is not included within its accessible name
- HTML: `<a class="openNav" role="button" tabindex="0" aria-label="Menu aufklappen" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="openNav"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R18: ARIA states are consistent with element semantics](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r18)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The attribute is prohibited for the element on which it is specified

#### Rule: [SIA-R2: HTML elements have a valid lang attribute](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r2)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The image does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/uploads/2021/02/Facebook.png" class="sidebar-img" width="36" height="36" />`
- XPath: `/img[@class="sidebar-img"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The image does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/uploads/2021/09/Messenger_Icon_2X.png" class="notify-img " width="26" height="27" />`
- XPath: `/img[@class="notify-img "]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R3: lang attribute has a valid language code](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r3)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<li id="id-menu-level-2-child-7" class="nav-item level-2 has-child  " data-child="menu-level-2-child-7">...</li>`
- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-7"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<ul id="id-menu-level-2-child-7" aria-hidden="true" role="menu" class="navbar-nav flex-column menu-level menu-level-2 menu-level-2-child-7" data-level="2">...</ul>`
- XPath: `/ul[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-7"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<li id="id-menu-level-2-child-8" class="nav-item level-2 has-child active current-ancestor" data-child="menu-level-2-child-8">...</li>`
- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-8"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<ul id="id-menu-level-2-child-8" aria-hidden="true" role="menu" class="navbar-nav flex-column menu-level menu-level-2 menu-level-2-child-8 show" data-level="2">...</ul>`
- XPath: `/ul[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-8"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<li id="id-menu-level-2-child-10" class="nav-item level-2 has-child  " data-child="menu-level-2-child-10">...</li>`
- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-10"]`

*... and 3 more failures for this rule*

- HTML: `<p class="pdf-file">PDF, 179.69 KB</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="pdf-file"]`

- HTML: `<p>...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

#### Rule: [SIA-R86: Page has a mechanism to bypass repeated blocks of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r86)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element is marked as decorative but is exposed
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-prev disabled">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="owl-prev disabled"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The element is marked as decorative but is exposed
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-next">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="owl-next"]`

### https://bayern.de/staatskanzlei/bayern-in-der-welt/

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="openNav" role="button" tabindex="0" aria-label="Menu aufklappen" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false">...</a>`

- XPath: `/a[@class="openSearch"]`

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The visible text content of the element is not included within its accessible name
- HTML: `<a class="openNav" role="button" tabindex="0" aria-label="Menu aufklappen" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="openNav"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R18: ARIA states are consistent with element semantics](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r18)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The attribute is prohibited for the element on which it is specified

#### Rule: [SIA-R2: HTML elements have a valid lang attribute](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r2)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The image does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/uploads/2021/02/Facebook.png" class="sidebar-img" width="36" height="36" />`
- XPath: `/img[@class="sidebar-img"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The image does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/uploads/2021/09/Messenger_Icon_2X.png" class="notify-img " width="26" height="27" />`
- XPath: `/img[@class="notify-img "]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R3: lang attribute has a valid language code](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r3)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<li id="id-menu-level-2-child-7" class="nav-item level-2 has-child  " data-child="menu-level-2-child-7">...</li>`
- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-7"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<ul id="id-menu-level-2-child-7" aria-hidden="true" role="menu" class="navbar-nav flex-column menu-level menu-level-2 menu-level-2-child-7" data-level="2">...</ul>`
- XPath: `/ul[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-7"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<li id="id-menu-level-2-child-8" class="nav-item level-2 has-child active current-ancestor" data-child="menu-level-2-child-8">...</li>`
- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-8"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<ul id="id-menu-level-2-child-8" aria-hidden="true" role="menu" class="navbar-nav flex-column menu-level menu-level-2 menu-level-2-child-8 show" data-level="2">...</ul>`
- XPath: `/ul[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-8"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<li id="id-menu-level-2-child-10" class="nav-item level-2 has-child  " data-child="menu-level-2-child-10">...</li>`
- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-10"]`

- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<ul id="id-menu-level-2-child-8" aria-hidden="true" role="menu" class="navbar-nav flex-column menu-level menu-level-2 menu-level-2-child-8" data-level="2">...</ul>`
- XPath: `/ul[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-8"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<li id="id-menu-level-2-child-10" class="nav-item level-2 has-child  " data-child="menu-level-2-child-10">...</li>`
- XPath: `/li[@id="id-menu-level-2-child-10"]`

*... and 3 more failures for this rule*

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The text is not included in a landmark region

- HTML: `<p>...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p>Porträt: Dr. Edmund Stoiber</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="des">Geboren am 28. September 1941 in Oberaudorf, Landk...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="des"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="title">Nach dem 2. juristischen Staatsexamen 1971</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="title"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="pdf-file">JPG, 1.15 MB</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="pdf-file"]`

## Detailed Failure Information (axe)

### https://bayern.de/

#### Rule: [aria-allowed-role](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/aria-allowed-role?application=playwright)
**Impact**: minor

**Failure 1:**
- Message: ARIA role should be appropriate for the element
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-prev disabled"><span aria-label="Bild zurueck">‹</span></button>`
- XPath: `#article-carousel-id-190561 > .owl-nav > .owl-prev[role="presentation"][type="button"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: ARIA role should be appropriate for the element
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-next"><span aria-label="Bild vor">› </span></button>`
- XPath: `#article-carousel-id-190561 > .owl-nav > .owl-next[role="presentation"][type="button"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: ARIA role should be appropriate for the element
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-prev disabled"><span aria-label="Bild zurueck">‹</span></button>`
- XPath: `#article-carousel-id-190022-3 > .owl-nav > .owl-prev[role="presentation"][type="button"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: ARIA role should be appropriate for the element
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-next"><span aria-label="Bild vor">› </span></button>`
- XPath: `#article-carousel-id-190022-3 > .owl-nav > .owl-next[role="presentation"][type="button"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: ARIA role should be appropriate for the element
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-prev"><div class="nav-btn prev-slide-media" aria-label="Vorheriger Slide/Element"></div></button>`
- XPath: `#press > .owl-nav > .owl-prev[role="presentation"][type="button"]`

*... and 3 more failures for this rule*

#### Rule: [aria-prohibited-attr](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/aria-prohibited-attr?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Elements must only use permitted ARIA attributes
- HTML: `<div id="news-result" aria-labelledby="emailfeld"></div>`
- XPath: `#news-result`

#### Rule: [image-alt](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/image-alt?application=playwright)
**Impact**: critical

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Images must have alternative text
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/uploads/2021/02/Facebook.png" class="sidebar-img" width="36" height="36">`
- XPath: `li:nth-child(1) > a[target="_blank"] > .sidebar-img[width="36"][height="36"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Images must have alternative text
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/uploads/2021/02/Youtube.png" class="sidebar-img" width="36" height="36">`
- XPath: `li:nth-child(2) > a[target="_blank"] > .sidebar-img[width="36"][height="36"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Images must have alternative text
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/uploads/2021/02/Instagram.png" class="sidebar-img" width="36" height="36">`
- XPath: `li:nth-child(3) > a[target="_blank"] > .sidebar-img[width="36"][height="36"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Images must have alternative text
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/Linkedin.png" class="sidebar-img" width="36" height="36">`
- XPath: `li:nth-child(4) > a[target="_blank"] > .sidebar-img[width="36"][height="36"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Images must have alternative text
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/uploads/2021/09/Messenger_Icon_2X.png" class="notify-img " width="26" height="27">`
- XPath: `.notify-img`

#### Rule: [link-name](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/link-name?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Links must have discernible text

#### Rule: [presentation-role-conflict](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/presentation-role-conflict?application=playwright)
**Impact**: minor

**Failure 2:**
- Message: ARIA role should be appropriate for the element
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-next"><span aria-label="Bild vor">› </span></button>`
- XPath: `.active.owl-item:nth-child(1) > .image-box > .image-box-img > .article > .article-img > .article-carousel[data-item="1"][data-mobile="1"] > .owl-nav > .owl-next[role="presentation"][type="button"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: ARIA role should be appropriate for the element
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-prev disabled"><span aria-label="Bild zurueck">‹</span></button>`
- XPath: `.active.owl-item:nth-child(2) > .image-box > .image-box-img > .article > .article-img > .article-carousel[data-item="1"][data-mobile="1"] > .owl-nav > .owl-prev[role="presentation"][type="button"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: ARIA role should be appropriate for the element
- HTML: `<button type="button" role="presentation" class="owl-next"><span aria-label="Bild vor">› </span></button>`
- XPath: `.active.owl-item:nth-child(2) > .image-box > .image-box-img > .article > .article-img > .article-carousel[data-item="1"][data-mobile="1"] > .owl-nav > .owl-next[role="presentation"][type="button"]`

- Message: Images must have alternative text

- XPath: `li:nth-child(1) > a[target="_blank"] > .sidebar-img[width="36"][height="36"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Images must have alternative text
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/uploads/2021/02/Youtube.png" class="sidebar-img" width="36" height="36">`
- XPath: `li:nth-child(2) > a[target="_blank"] > .sidebar-img[width="36"][height="36"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Images must have alternative text
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/uploads/2021/02/Instagram.png" class="sidebar-img" width="36" height="36">`
- XPath: `li:nth-child(3) > a[target="_blank"] > .sidebar-img[width="36"][height="36"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Images must have alternative text
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/Linkedin.png" class="sidebar-img" width="36" height="36">`
- XPath: `li:nth-child(4) > a[target="_blank"] > .sidebar-img[width="36"][height="36"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Images must have alternative text
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/uploads/2021/09/Messenger_Icon_2X.png" class="notify-img " width="26" height="27">`
- XPath: `.notify-img`

#### Rule: [region](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/region?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate

**Failure 1:**
- Message: All page content should be contained by landmarks
- HTML: `<div class="cookie-text">`
- XPath: `.cookie-text`

### https://bayern.de/staatsregierung/ministerpraesidentenkonferenz/

#### Rule: [aria-prohibited-attr](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/aria-prohibited-attr?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Elements must only use permitted ARIA attributes
- HTML: `<div id="news-result" aria-labelledby="emailfeld"></div>`
- XPath: `#news-result`

#### Rule: [image-alt](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/image-alt?application=playwright)
**Impact**: critical

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Images must have alternative text
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/uploads/2021/02/Facebook.png" class="sidebar-img" width="36" height="36">`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Images must have alternative text
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/uploads/2021/02/Instagram.png" class="sidebar-img" width="36" height="36">`

#### Rule: [link-in-text-block](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/link-in-text-block?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Links must be distinguishable without relying on color
- HTML: `<a title="Externer Link: Mit Klick auf diesen Link verlassen Sie die Webseite www.bayern.de" href="https://www.rlp.de/mpk" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Rheinland-Pfalz</a>`
- XPath: `a[href$="mpk"][rel="noopener"][target="_blank"]`

### https://bayern.de/staatsregierung/regierungserklaerungen-uebersicht/

**Impact**: critical

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Buttons must have discernible text
- HTML: `<button class="btn btn-primary" type="submit" id="suchbutton">`
- XPath: `#suchbutton`

#### Rule: [image-alt](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/image-alt?application=playwright)
**Impact**: critical

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Images must have alternative text
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/themes/bayernde/assets/images/svg/Calendar.svg" border="0">`
- XPath: `#myDatepicker > .date > .group > .icon.red[aria-label="Datumsauswahl anzeigen"] > img[border="0"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Images must have alternative text
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/themes/bayernde/assets/images/svg/Calendar.svg" border="0">`
- XPath: `#myDatepicker2 > .date > .group > .icon.red[aria-label="Datumsauswahl anzeigen"] > img[border="0"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Images must have alternative text
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/uploads/2021/02/Facebook.png" class="sidebar-img" width="36" height="36">`
- XPath: `li:nth-child(1) > a[target="_blank"] > .sidebar-img[width="36"][height="36"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Images must have alternative text
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/uploads/2021/02/Youtube.png" class="sidebar-img" width="36" height="36">`
- XPath: `li:nth-child(2) > a[target="_blank"] > .sidebar-img[width="36"][height="36"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Images must have alternative text
- HTML: `<img src="/wp-content/uploads/2021/02/Instagram.png" class="sidebar-img" width="36" height="36">`
- XPath: `li:nth-child(3) > a[target="_blank"] > .sidebar-img[width="36"][height="36"]`
